<script type="text/javascript">
    function setEdition(target, d_p) {
        // set cookie for default edition
        //document.cookie ="myEdition="+target+"; expires=Fri, 1 Jan 2038 01:23:45 GMT; path=/";
        if(!d_p) d_p = 'http';
        var days=90;
        var date = new Date();
        date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
        var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
        var currentTime = (new Date).getTime();
        document.cookie = "editionPostpone="+currentTime+expires+"; path=/";

        ga('allSitesTracker.send', 'event', 'Edition Redirect Popup', 'System Recommend', 'Redirect to '+target+'.investing.com');
		setTimeout('document.location = "'+d_p+'://'+ target +'.investing.com?ref=www"', 500);
	}

    function postponeEdition(days, reason) {
        if (days!=14) days=1;
        //$('#editionLoading').removeClass("displayNone").addClass("inlineblock");
        // set cookie for days not to show bar again
        //change time from 7 days to 14 (2 weeks), Gil Palikaras, JIRA-26314
        var date = new Date();
        date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
        var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
        var currentTime = (new Date).getTime();
        document.cookie = "editionPostpone="+currentTime+expires+"; path=/";
        closeTopAlert();
        ga('allSitesTracker.send', 'event', 'Edition Redirect Popup', 'System Recommend', reason);
    }
    function closeTopAlert(){
        $('#topAlertBarContainer').fadeOut('fast');
    }

    $(document).ready (function(){
                var timer = setInterval(function() {
            if ($('#mainPopUpBannerDIV').is( ":hidden" )==true) {
                clearInterval(timer);
                //openTopAlert(2000);
            }
        }, 200);
            });
</script>			<!-- /GEO POPUP -->
		</div>

<script type="text/javascript">

  	window.ecPrinted = {
		prn: 'printed',
		base64Images: null,

		preparePrintIcons: function() {
			var $els = window.ecPrinted.revertPrintIcons();
			$('#ecEventsTable')
				.find('.grayEmptyBullishIcon').data('img_key', 'imp_bull0').end()
				.find('.grayFullBullishIcon').data('img_key', 'imp_bull1');
			$els.each(function(i) {
				var $el = $els.eq(i);
				var m = $el.css('background-image').match(/url\((.*)\)/);
				if (m && !$el.is('.' + window.ecPrinted.prn)) {
					var left;
					var top;
					var img_url;
					var $img = $('<img>');
					var bp = $el.css('background-position');
					if (bp) {
						bp = bp.split(' ');
						left = bp[0];
						top = bp[1];
					} else {
						left = $el.css('background-position-x');
						top = $el.css('background-position-y');
					}
					if (window.ecPrinted.base64Images) {
						img_url = window.ecPrinted.base64Images[$el.data('img_key')];
						top = 1;
						left = 1;
					} else {
						img_url = m[1].replace(/"/g, '');
					}
					$img.prop('src', img_url).css({position: 'absolute', top: top, left: left}).addClass(window.ecPrinted.prn);
					$el.addClass(window.ecPrinted.prn).append($img).css({position: 'relative', backgroundImage: 'none', width: '16px', height: '16px'});
				}
			});

			$('.diamondNewIcon').css({backgroundColor: 'transparent'});
			$('.chatOuterWrapper').css({visibility: 'hidden'});
			setTimeout(window.ecPrinted.revertPrintIcons, 5000);
		},

		revertPrintIcons: function() {
			var $els = $('#economicCalendarData, #ecoCalLegend').find('.ceFlags, .grayFullBullishIcon, .grayEmptyBullishIcon, .audioIconNew, .smallGrayP, .sandClock');
			$('.diamondNewIcon').css({backgroundColor: ''});
            $('.chatOuterWrapper').css({visibility: 'visible'});
			$els.each(function() {
				var $el = $(this);
				if ($el.is('.' + window.ecPrinted.prn)) {
					$el.css({backgroundImage: ''}).removeClass(window.ecPrinted.prn)
						.find('img.' + window.ecPrinted.prn).remove();
				}
			});
			return $els;
		}
	}
</script>

<script>
    (function(window, $, components) {
        'use strict';

        var $timezonePopup = $("#economicCurrentTimePop");
        var $scrollableList = $timezonePopup.find('.js-scrollable-block');
        var $timezone = $("#timeZone");
        var $clock = $('#currentTime');
        var $timezoneOffset = $('#timeZoneGmtOffsetFormatted');
        var $options = $scrollableList.find('li');
        var $currentOption;

        var timezonePopup;
        var autoUpdateMode = true;
        var clockDateTime;
        var lastLocalClock;
        var timerId;
        var currentValue = $timezone.val();
        var optionsIdsPrefix = 'liTz';
        var callbacks = [];

        $(document).ready(function() {
            timezonePopup = new components.TooltipPopup($timezonePopup);
        });

        function makeDoubleCharsNumber(num) {
            return (num > 9) ? num : ('0' + num.toString());
        }

        function getClockTimeForView(dateObj) {
            return makeDoubleCharsNumber(dateObj.getHours()) + ':' + makeDoubleCharsNumber(dateObj.getMinutes());
        }

        function updateClockOnView() {
            $clock.text(getClockTimeForView(clockDateTime));
        }

        function getRemainingSecondsFromClock() {
            return (60 - clockDateTime.getSeconds()) * 1000;
        }

        function updateClockObj(datetime) {
            var prevSeconds = clockDateTime.getSeconds();
            clockDateTime = new Date(datetime);
            if(prevSeconds > clockDateTime.getSeconds()) {
                components.Timezone.updateClock(clockDateTime);
            } else {
                runInterval();
            }
        }

        function runInterval() {
            lastLocalClock = Date.now();
            var remainSecondsFromClock = Math.min(getRemainingSecondsFromClock(), 5000);
            timerId = setTimeout(function () {
                updateClockObj(clockDateTime.valueOf() + (Date.now() - lastLocalClock));
            }, remainSecondsFromClock);
        }

        function scrollPopupContentToCurrentTZ() {
            $currentOption.addClass('selected');

            $scrollableList
                .scrollTop(0) // reset list scroll position
                .scrollTop($currentOption.offset().top - $timezonePopup.offset().top);

            // remove class selected when hovering
            // binded to options and not to list because list includes the scrollbar of itself.
            $options.one('mouseenter.scrollPopup', function() {
                $currentOption.removeClass('selected');
                $options.off('mouseenter.scrollPopup');
            });

        }

        components.Timezone = {
            subscribe: function(fn) {
                if(typeof fn === 'function') callbacks.push(fn);
                return this;
            },
            getTimezone: function() {
                return currentValue;
            },
            getClockEl: function() {
                return $clock;
            },
            setClockAutoUpdate: function(bool) {
                autoUpdateMode = !!bool;
                return this;
            },
            setClock: function(datetimeObj) {
                $clock.text(getClockTimeForView(datetimeObj));
                return this;
            },
            updateClock: function (newDateTimeFormatted) {
                clockDateTime = new Date(newDateTimeFormatted);
                updateClockOnView();
                if (timerId) {
                    clearTimeout(timerId);
                }
                if(autoUpdateMode) {
                    runInterval();
                }
                return this;
            },
            setTimezoneOffset: function(str) {
                $timezoneOffset.html(str);
                return this;
            }
        };

        $("#economicCurrentTime").click(function (eventObject) {
            if (timezonePopup.isShown()) return;
            timezonePopup.show();

            scrollPopupContentToCurrentTZ();

            eventObject.stopPropagation();
        });

        //On selection of a timezone set the hidden select option accordingly.
        //close the selection div. submit the form and reload the events table.
        //update the current time.
        $options
            .click(function () {
                var $this = $(this);
                var optionValue = $this.attr("id").substr(optionsIdsPrefix.length);

                //Select the pressed timeZone
                currentValue = optionValue;
                $currentOption = $this;
                $timezone.val(optionValue);

                //Set the string displaying the time and timezone
                timezonePopup.hide();

                callbacks.forEach(function (fn) {
                    fn(currentValue);
                });
            })
            .each(function () {
                var $this = $(this);
                var optionValue = $this.attr("id").substr(optionsIdsPrefix.length);

                if(currentValue === optionValue) {
                    $currentOption = $this;
                    return false;
                }
            });

        // init clock auto update
        components.Timezone.updateClock(components.Timezone.getClockEl().attr('data-datetime'));

    })(window, jQuery, window.components = window.components || {});
</script>		
</form>

<script>
    
//declare variables
var calendarType = 'economicCalendar';
var datePickerFirstDayOfWeek = siteData.datepicker.firstDay;

//create new calendarFilters object
var calendarFilters = new CalendarFiltersWidget('economic', '{"country":["25","32","6","37","72","22","17","39","14","10","35","43","36","110","11","26","12","4","5","56"],"time":"timeRemain","category":[],"importance":[]}');   

$('[id^="timeFrame_"]').on('click', function(e){
	var tabName = $(this).attr('id');
	calendarFilters.timeFrameFilter(tabName.replace('timeFrame_',''));
})


$(document).ready(function(){

	/* all functions and variables for datePickers */
    var datePickerFrom = calendarFilters.strToDate('2020-04-07');
    var datePickerTo = calendarFilters.strToDate('2020-04-07');
    if (calendarType == 'holidayCalendar'){
    	datePickerFrom = new Date().addDays(-1);
    	datePickerTo = new Date().addMonths(3);
    }

    $('#datePickerToggleBtn').click(function (e) {
		if(!$('#'+calendarType+'Loading:visible').length){
			return true;
		}
		e.preventDefault();
		e.stopImmediatePropagation();
		e.stopPropagation();
		return false;
	});

    var myPicker = new MyDatePicker('#picker','#widgetFieldDateRange',siteData.datepicker.format,datePickerFrom,datePickerTo,siteData.datepicker.translations);
    myPicker.setFirstDay(siteData.datepicker.firstDay);
    myPicker.setDayNames(siteData.datepicker.dayNames);

    myPicker.setRtl(siteData.htmlDirection);
    myPicker.setMonthNamesShort(siteData.datepicker.monthNamesShort);
    myPicker.setMonthNames(siteData.datepicker.monthNames);

    myPicker.setApplyButtonText(siteData.datepicker.applyButton);
    myPicker.setPickerType(2);
    myPicker.setTrigger('#datePickerToggleBtn');
    myPicker.alignToCenterOfDiv('#'+calendarType+'Data');
	    myPicker.create();

    $('[id^=timeFrame_]').click(function () {
        $('#datePickerToggleBtn').removeClass('toggled');
    });

	$(myPicker.input).on('onClose', function (e, selectedText, currentInstance, dates, applyBtn) {
        if (applyBtn) {
        	var dates = $.datepicker._getFromToDates($.datepicker._curInst,'yy-mm-dd');
            if(typeof calendarFilters !='undefined') {
                calendarFilters.datePickerFilter(dates.dateFromStr, dates.dateToStr);
            }
        }
    });
})

</script>

	function checkAds(){

		function isIE() {
			var ua = window.navigator.userAgent;
			var trident = ua.indexOf('Trident/');
			var edge = ua.indexOf('Edge/');
			var msie = ua.indexOf('MSIE ');
			return Math.max(msie,edge,trident)>0;

		}

		var isIE = isIE();
		var isChrome = /Chrome/.test(navigator.userAgent) && /Google Inc/.test(navigator.vendor) && !isIE;
		var isFireFox = /Firefox/.test(navigator.userAgent);
		var isSafari = /Safari/.test(navigator.userAgent) && /Apple Computer/.test(navigator.vendor);

<script>
//disabled is a temporary argument for testing purposes 
var BoxesEvents = function($,ga,disabled)
{
	var e_stack = []; //each event is pushed to this stack
	//this objcet links urls to event types
    var boxes = {"side_central_banks":"centralbanks","webmaster_tools":"wmt","Most_Popular_News":"mostpop","broker_promotions":"sb_promotions","marketMoversBoxWrapper":"sb_marketmovers","QBS_2_inner":"sb_indices","QBS_3_inner":"sb_commodities","QBS_1_inner":"sb_forex","QBS_4_inner":"sb_bonds","TSB_1_inner":"tsb_fx","TSB_2_inner":"tsb_commodities","TSB_3_inner":"tsb_indices","TSB_4_inner":"tsb_stocks"};

    var resume_click_event = function(ev)
    {
    	if (ev['link']==='') {return;}
        window.location.href = ev['link'];
    }
    
    
	var register_events = function()
	{
	    for (var id in boxes)
	    {
		    (function(id){
			    var _$b = $('#'+id);
			    if (_$b.length < 1) {return;}
			    
			    //box click event
			    _$b.mouseup(function(e){
					if (e.button === 2) {return true;} //right mouse button
					var middleMouse = e.button === 1;
				    if (!middleMouse) {e.preventDefault();}
				    var box_event = boxes[id];
				    e_stack.push({'event':box_event,'link':''});
				    var ce = null; //current event 
				    //function creator
				    var callbackCreate = function(data) {return function() {resume_click_event(data);}}
		            var hitCallback = null;
		            
				    while(ce = e_stack.pop())
				    {
						if (ce['link'].substr(0,10) === "javascript") {continue;}//if the link is javascript call ignore it
						hitCallback = middleMouse ? function(){} : callbackCreate(ce);
				    	//if a link with no event do nothing
					    if (ce['event'] == '') {hitCallback(); return true;}
						
				    					        window.ga('t0.send',{
                            'hitType': 'event',          
                            'eventCategory': 'side-box-events',
                            'eventAction': ce['event'], 
                            'eventValue' : 1,
                            'hitCallback': hitCallback //resume click event
				            }
				        );
				        //fallback if ga doesn't work
				        window.setTimeout(hitCallback,1500);
				    }
				    return middleMouse;
			    });
			    
			    //link event 
                _$b.on('mouseup','a',function(e){
					if (e.button === 2) {return true;} //right mouse button
                	e.preventDefault();
					var url = this.getAttribute('href');
					var event = this.getAttribute('data-gae');
					e_stack.push({'event':'','link':url});
					if (event)
					{
						e_stack.pop();
						e_stack.push({'event':event,'link':url});
					} 
				  });
    	        
		    })(id);
	    }		   	
	};
	
    var init = function()
    {
        if (disabled) {return;}
        if (typeof $ !== 'function') {return;}
        if (typeof ga !== 'function') {return;}
        register_events();
    }();
}(window.jQuery,window.ga,false);
</script>
